NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

Apr. 13, 2011]

TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE

767

IN THE MATTER OF COMPANIES ACT, 1956
IN THE MATTER OF MADRAS PRUDENT INVESTMENT SERVICES PRIVATE LIMITED
At an Extraordinary General Meeting of the Company held on 11th April, 2011 at 12-C, Vaidyaraman Street, T. Nagar,
Chennai-600 017, the following resolution was passed to voluntarily wind up Madras Prudent Investment Services Private
Limited.
Resolved that having regard to the declaration of solvency dated 14th March, 2011, made by the Board of Directors of the
Company under Section 488 of the Companies Act, 1956, stating that the Company would be able to pay its debts in full within
a period of three years from the date of declaration thereof, the Company having its Registered Office at 12-C, Vaidyaraman
Street, T. Nagar, Chennai-600 017, be wound up voluntarily, pursuant to Section 484 (1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956.
Chennai,
28th March 2011.

S. MUTHIAH,
Director.

It is hereby informed to public at large that, I, P. Sivakumar, Managing Partner of VSN GALVANISING AND ENGINEERING, Office and
industry at Plot No. 126 to 131 and RO3, Sidco Women Industrial Estate, Valavanthankottai, Thuvakudi, Tiruchirappalli-15,
do hereby publish that,
One N. Vijayalakshmi, aged about 37 years, wife of R. Nallendran, erstwhile Managing Partner of above firm had resigned
from above post on 23rd January 2010 and relieved from firm publically by Rs. 20,000,00/- on 10th December 2010.
Hence, I and one T.R. Velmurugan were partners of VSN GALVANISING AND ENGINEERING from 10th December 2010.
Therefore, we declare and inform to public at large to desist from N. Vijayalakshmi in any manner related to our firm’s
business activities or believing her as Managing Partner.

Tiruchirappalli,
28th March 2011.

For VSN GALVANISING AND ENGINEERING,
P. SIVAKUMAR,
Partner.
